The noodles are not suitable for making cold dishes.

posted:Posted April 8, 2024
msg:I went there during the cherry blossom season. I didn't book Sakura Villa. This hotel is a very good second choice. It is right next to the Lihu Ferris Wheel. The hotel has a boat that goes directly to Yuantouzhu Chongshan Wharf. It is smooth to enter the park without any delay. After entering the park, I went directly to take the sightseeing bus (free buses need to queue up, and those who are too lazy to wait are recommended to give priority to the sightseeing bus). I bought a 40-yuan ticket and went straight to the Sakura Valley.
After browsing in a clockwise direction, I took the bus back to the gate. I didn't catch the hotel's return boat (the last one at 16:00 was too early, and 18:00 was the most suitable). I took the Leyou No. 1 bus at the exit, which cost 5 yuan per person. I didn't wait for a few minutes and got off at Liyuan one stop. It was very smooth and didn't hurt my legs.
The hotel's buffet is also recommended. I stayed in Zone B, a lake view room, which is quite new and large. The balcony is very pleasant to look at Taihu Lake.

posted:Posted April 15, 2024
msg:I have to give a negative review. Leaving aside the hardware, the quality of the receptionists at this hotel is extremely poor. I booked three twin rooms in Building A. After going through the formalities, the front desk clerk said that the three rooms all faced north. I said at that time that I was taking two 80-year-olds and a child out, hoping to change to a south-facing room. The waiter said that the room you booked was facing north. I said that the room orientation was not marked on the booking page. The waiter argued that you didn't look carefully. I opened the Ctrip booking page on the spot, and it only marked double and twin rooms. The waiter was speechless and called another man (probably at the lobby manager level) to listen. What happened was that our double bed faced south and the twin bed faced north. After hearing this, I still gave the same answer. The Ctrip booking page did not indicate north and south. The man said that was how we determined the direction of the room. I was being unreasonable. Then I ask, are you also misleading consumers by not marking the direction of the room? The man couldn't answer and said that there are no rooms now, otherwise you can make a new reservation. I said since there is no room, why should I make a new reservation? After negotiating for a long time, the man said I would upgrade one of your rooms to Building B. I asked what to do with the other two rooms? The man looked like he was taking advantage of others, so I was too tired after driving for a long time and didn't bother to argue with him, so I took my room card and entered the room. The upgraded room was actually being renovated upstairs, and the wall was being smashed constantly, making it impossible to rest, so I went downstairs to ask him to change rooms. The man answered me, just in time for you to hear. After hearing this, I was really speechless, as if I was deliberately blackmailing him. A colleague next to him said that I would change your room to another room. At the same time, he sent fruits to all three of my rooms. Thank her! However, the hardware problems of the room were exposed again. It may be that corners were cut during the renovation. The room was extremely not soundproof, and the voices in the next room sounded like they were in the same room. In short, don't come to this hotel when you come to Wuxi. The only advantage is that it is by Taihu Lake. The breakfast is quite rich, but the rest is useless. The JAL and Intercontinental airlines in the city are really much better than here!

msg:After 2 months, I came to Wuxi with my parents again. This time I chose Wuxi Junlai Lakeside Hotel. I will briefly write about my stay experience.

1. The service is warm.
1) Introduce service types. After we checked in, we received a call from hotel staff manager Zhang Yi. Manager Zhang Yi introduced us to the services the hotel can provide, such as butler service (meal delivery, takeout delivery) and other services. We bought fruits and snacks on the takeout platform. Manager Zhang Yi would confirm the purchase content with me in advance to avoid getting the wrong food, and then the hotel staff would "deliver it to my door" in a timely manner.
2) Handle emergencies. After returning to the room after breakfast, I found that I didn't bring my room card. After contacting Manager Zhang Yi, Manager Zhang Yi immediately notified the relevant staff to open the door for us. The waiting process was short and did not affect the experience and schedule.
      Manager Zhang Yi's warm service and powerful handling made our trip to Wuxi feel warm, comfortable and considerate.

2. The site selection is unique.
       As the hotel's introduction says: "Dominating the landscape of Lihu Lake, a corner of Taihu Lake." This time I chose a lake view room. The room faces Xishi Village and has a panoramic view of Li Lake. These two days were mainly cloudy and cloudy. In the morning, the hazy mountains and clouds were intertwined, forming an unpredictable and hazy scenery. The hotel is designed in a garden style, allowing people to find a place for their souls to live in the city. It is also in line with people's current concept of "not only wanting city lights, but also retaining the starlight of the countryside".

3. Food diversity.
1) Chinese restaurant. The Chinese restaurant mainly focuses on Wuxi local cuisine. My parents and I tasted dishes such as Wuxi Sauce Pork Ribs, Xiao Long Bao, Shuangdong Gluten, and Taihu Sanbai. Among them, the shiitake mushrooms grown in Shuangdong Gluten are juicy and delicious, and the gluten is chewy, leaving a deep impression on people. Secondly, the cooking method of sauced pork ribs may be to boil them first and then pour the sauce. This cooking method may lead to a woody taste, so , slightly inferior. Others are quite satisfactory, so I won‚Äôt comment on them one by one.
2) Rose Garden. The breakfast buffet is in the Rose Garden, offering a variety of choices such as Chinese and Western food. As a Shanghainese, tofu pudding is indispensable in the morning. The soy sauce of tofu pudding is very colorful and tastes good. Overall, it is quite satisfactory.
      This time I came to Wuxi with my parents to fulfill my vows. The trip was quite rushed. After staying for 2 days, I hurried back to Shanghai. I hope they can slow down, feel life and experience the world in the future.

Advantages: 1. The location is excellent, Liyuan is just across the wall, and there is a Ferris wheel amu*****t park next to it. The hotel is located by the Lihu Lake. You can enjoy the wide lake view by yourself in the garden, and it is very convenient to take a taxi. 2. Excellent catering, rich variety of buffets, Chinese restaurant tastes wrong, there is also a black pearl, all three are good value for money, all three restaurants are full during the May Day holiday. 3. The service is enthusiastic. Every service staff encountered in the restaurant, concierge, and front desk is full of enthusiasm. It can be seen that every staff member does their best to help the guests.
Disadvantages: 1. The overall transportation capacity is insufficient, such as cleaning the guest room late, and the buffet cannot be replenished, etc. I believe there will be no such problems in normal times. 2. The facilities are a bit old. The suite has only one toilet and one washbasin, which is a little inconvenient.
Suggestions: 1. Book a lake-view room on the 8th floor or above. It is better to have a balcony. From the room, you can see the beautiful scenery of Lihu Lake, and you can also see Liyuan from the perspective of God. 2. The hotel can book tickets and cruise ships for several scenic spots, without having to queue at the ticket office.
All in all it was a pleasant trip.
